    "7": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">7</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua ciangin Siampi Ukpa in, “Hih thute a maan mah ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Stephen in, “Pate le sanggamte aw, ka thugen na ngai un. A pa a sih khit ciangin tua mun panin tu laitak a na teenna uh leitang ah a lal hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua gamah Pasian in ama luah dingin a khepek ngakh nading nangawn leitang a pia kei hi. Tu in note in tua a Dikpa a lehhekte le a thatte na suakzo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"53\"><sup data-verseid=\"53\">&nbsp;<!-- -->53<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"53\">Note in vantungmite tungtawn a hong kipia thukham ngah napi in na zui kei uh hi,” ci in a gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"54\"><sup data-verseid=\"54\">&nbsp;<!-- -->54<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"54\">Amaute in hih thute a zak uh ciangin a lung uh so a, a ha uh a gawisan uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"55\"><sup data-verseid=\"55\">&nbsp;<!-- -->55<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"55\">Ahih hangin Stephen in Kha Siangtho tawh kidim in vantung a ettoh leh Pasian vangliatna le Pasian taklam a a ding Zeisu a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"56\"><sup data-verseid=\"56\">&nbsp;<!-- -->56<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"56\">Amah in, “En un! Vantung kihong a, Pasian taklam ah Mihing Tapa dinga om ka mu hi!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"57\"><sup data-verseid=\"57\">&nbsp;<!-- -->57<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"57\">Tua ciangin amaute nakpi in kiko uh a, a bil uh humkawm in ama lamah lungsim kituak in a hong tai uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"58\"><sup data-verseid=\"58\">&nbsp;<!-- -->58<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"58\">Khua nawlah amah kaikhia in suang tawh a denglum uh hi. Tua a denglum mite in Saul a kici tangval khat khephung ah a puante uh a koih uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"59\"><sup data-verseid=\"59\">&nbsp;<!-- -->59<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"59\">Suang tawh a den laitak un Stephen in, “Topa Zeisu aw, ka kha hong la in,” ci in Pasian kiangah thu a ngen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"60\"><sup data-verseid=\"60\">&nbsp;<!-- -->60<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"60\">Tua khit ciangin amah khukdin a, “Topa aw, hih mawhna amaute tungah na suan kei in,” ci in nakpitak in a kiko khit ciangin a si hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "8": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">8</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tu in Stephen a kithahna thu ah Saul zong a thukim hi.     "9": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">9</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Hih hun sungin Saul in Topa nungzuite thah dingin a sawm hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ahih manin hih Lampi thu a um numei pasal a muh peuhpeuh manin Jerusalem khuapi ah a puak theih nadingin Siampi Ukpa kiangah pai in, Damascus khuapi a kikhopna inn ukte a lah ding phalna lai a ngen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Amah hong kuankhia a Damascus khuapi a tunkuan in thakhat in vantung pan khuavak khat ama kimkot ah a tang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua ciangin amah lei ah puksuk a, “Saul aw, Saul aw, banghang in hong bawlsia na hi hiam?” ci a, hopihna awging khat a za hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua ciangin amah in, “Topa aw, nang kua na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Topa in, “Na hong bawlsiat Zeisu ka hi hi. Ciangzum sui lecin nang aa dingin na mahmah ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua ciangin amah in lamdangsa mahmah in a ciling a, “Topa aw, bang hih dinga hong deih na hi hiam?” a ci hi. Tua ciangin Topa in ama kiangah, “Tho inla khua sungah lut in. Na hih ding teng hong kigen ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Saul tawh a zinkhawm mite in tua awging a zak uh hangin kuamah mu lo uh ahih manin gen ding mel thei loin a dingcip uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Saul zong leilak pan tho in a khuadak hangin kuamah a muthei kei hi. Amaute in a khutah lenin Damascus khuapi sungah a lutpih uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Amah in khuamu lo, an nelo, tui dawn loin ni thum sung a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Tu in Damascus khuapi sungah Ananias a kici nungzuipa khat om a, a mangmuhna sungah Topa in, “Ananias aw,” ci in a sam hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Hihlai ah ka om hi, Topa aw,” ci in a dawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Topa in, “Dingkhia inla, ‘Tang,’ a kici kongzing ah va pai in. Judas inn ah Tarsus khua mi Saul a kici pa va kankhia in. En in, amah thungen in a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Thu a nget laitak in mang mu a, Ananias a kici mi khat ama kiangah hong pai in khua a muhkik theih nadingin ama tungah a khut hong nga ding hi cih thu a mu zo hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua ciangin Ananias in, “Topa aw, hihpa in Jerusalem khuapi a om nangma misiangthote bawlsia mahmah hi cih mi tampi tung panin ka zazo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Hih khua ah zong nangma min a suang khempeuh a mat theih nadingin siampi liante kiang panin phalna a ngah khinzo hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Ahih hangin Topa in, “Va pai in. Gentile‑te, kumpite le Israel tate mai ah ka min a genkhia dinga ka teel, keima vanzat khat ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Keima min hangin a thuak ding gimna tampi ka laklai ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Ananias zong pai in tua inn sungah va lut a, Saul tungah a khut nga in, “Ka sanggampa Saul aw, khua na muhkik nading le Kha Siangtho tawh na kidim nadingin nong paina lampi a hong kilang Topa Zeisu in kei hong sawl hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tua ciangin Saul mit panin ngalip tawh a kibang na khat thakhat in kia a, khua a muthei pah hi. Tua ciangin amah tho in tui a kiphum hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">An a nek khit ciangin a tha a dimkik hi. Tua khit ciangin Damascus khuapi a om nungzuite tawh tawmvei sung Saul a omkhawm hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Kikhopna inn ah Saul pai a, “Zeisu in Pasian Tapa ahi hi,” ci in Khazih thu a hilh pah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Ama thugen a za khempeuh in lamdangsa mahmah uh a, “Hihpa in Jerusalem khuapi sunga Zeisu min a suangte a bawlsiapa hilo ahi hiam? Hih khua ah zong tua mite manin, siampi liante kiangah a puak dinga hong pai hilo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Ahih hangin Saul thakhauh semsem a, Zeisu in Khazih ahi hi ci in teltak in lak ahih manin Damascus khuapi a teeng Judah mite lungsim a patausak mahmah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Ni tampi khit ciangin Judah mite in Saul thah dingin a vaihawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Ahih hangin Saul in amaute vaihawmna a thei hi. Amaute in amah a thah theih nadingun kongpi ah sun le zan in a pang uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Tua ahih manin nungzuite in zan laitak in Saul paipih uh a, bawmpi sungah koihin kulhpi pua lamah a khaisuk uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Jerusalem khuapi ah Saul a tun ciangin nungzuite tawh kipawl ding a hanciam hangin amah nungzui suak khin cih thu um zolo uh ahih manin a vekpi un a kihta uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Ahih hangin Barnabas in sawltakte kiangah amah paipih a, lampi ah Topa a muhna, Topa in amah a hopihna le Damascus khuapi sungah Zeisu min tawh hangtak a thu a hilhnate a gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Tua ciangin Saul in Jerusalem ah amaute tawh kikhawl a, sungtum pusuak in a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Amah in Topa Zeisu min tawh hangtak in thu a gen hi. Greek dan a zui Judah mite tawh thu kinial uh a, amaute in amah thah a sawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Sanggamte in hihthu a theih uh ciangin Caesarea khua ah amah kha uh a, tua panin Tarsus khua ah a paisak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Tua hun in Judea gam a kipan Galilee gam le Samaria gam khempeuh a om pawlpite lungmuangtak in om uh a, tha a ngah uh hi. Topa kihtakna le Kha Siangtho thapiakna tawh kalsuan uh a, a pung semsem uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tu in Peter khualzin kawikawi a, Lydda khua‑a a teeng misiangthote kiangah a hong tung hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Tua khua ah Aeneas a kici mipa khat a om hi. Amah a pumzaw ahih manin kum giat sung lupna tung ngakin a om khat ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Peter in ama kiangah, “Aeneas aw, Zeisu Khazih in nang hong damsak zo hi. Tho inla, na lupna zial in,” a ci hi. Amah zong thakhat in a tho pah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Tua hi a, Lydda khua le Sharon zanglei a teeng mi khempeuh in tua pa a muh uh ciangin Topa lamah a kikhel uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Tu in Joppa khua ah Tabitha, Greek pau in Dorcas a kici nungzui numei khat a om hi. Tua nu in mizawngte huhin thupha a bawl tawntung numei khat ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Tua laitak in amah cina in a si hi. A luang a sil khit uh ciangin inndei tungnung ah a sial uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Joppa khua le Lydda khua kinai ahih manin tua khua ah Peter om hi cih thu nungzuite in a zak khitsa uh ahi hi. Peter sam dingin mi nih sawl uh a, thakhat in a hong pai pah nadingin a thumsak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">Peter zong dingin amaute tawh a paikhawm hi. A tun ciangin inndei tungnung ah a kahtohpih uh hi. Meigong khempeuh Peter kiangah dingin kap uh a, Dorcas in a nuntak lai‑a a khuisak nikteen puansilhte a lak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Peter in amaute khempeuh a pusuahsak khit ciangin khukdin in thu a ngen hi. Tua khit ciangin misi luang lamah kihei in, “Tabitha aw, tho in,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin tua nu a mit hong hak a, Peter a muh ciangin a tho hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Tua ciangin Peter in a khut khakin dingsak a, misiangthote le meigongte samin a nungtakik Dorcas a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Joppa khua sungteng ah tua thu kizel a, mi tampi in Topa a um uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"43\"><sup data-verseid=\"43\">&nbsp;<!-- -->43<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"43\">Joppa khua ah Peter ni tampi taam a, savun khuipa Simon inn ah a kinga hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp;     "10": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">10</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Caesarea khua ah Cornelius kici mi khat om a, Italy galkaphonɠ sungah galkap 100 ukpa khat ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">A innkuanpih khempeuh tawh Pasian thu hahkat in Pasian a kihta mi khat ahi hi. Mizawngte tungah cinghtak in huhna pia a, Pasian kiangah thu a ngen tawntung mi khat zong ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Ni khat, nai kua pawlin mang mu a, “Cornelius aw!” ci in a hopih Pasian vantungmi khat teltak in a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Amah in vantungmi limtak in a et ciangin lau a, “Bang ahi hiam, topa aw?” a ci hi. Vantungmi in ama kiangah, “Na thungetna le mizawngte na huhna Pasian in hong thei khinzo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tu in Joppa khua ah mi sawl inla, Peter a kici Simon samsak in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Amah in tuipi gei‑a a teeng savun khuipa Simon inn ah a om hi. Amah in na hih ding teng a hong hilh ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Amah a hopih vantungmi a paikhiat khit ciangin Cornelius in a innsung nasemte nih le a kisapna teng a sepsak den Pasian thu a hahkat galkap khat a sam hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">A thuteng a hilhcian khit ciangin Joppa khua ah amaute a paisak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">A zingciang in amaute zinkhia uh a, Joppa khua a tunkuan uh nai guk hun pawlin Peter zong thungen dingin innkhumzang ah a kahto hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Amah a gilkial mahmah a, an a lunggulh hi. Ahi zongin ankuang a bawl laitak un Peter in mangmu a,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">van kihong in puanzapi tawh a kibang kiuli a nei, a kiu ciat ah a kikhihsa in vantung pan a kikhai, ama lamah hong kiasuk a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua sungah leitung a om khe li nei ganhing namkimte, gamsate, a bokvak ganhingte le vana leng vasate a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua laitak in aw khat hong ging a, “Peter aw, tho in, tuate go inla ne in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Ahih hangin Peter in, “Topa aw, ka ne peuhmah kei ding hi! Banghang hiam cihleh a nekhuailo le a sianglo na khat beek ka ne ngei kei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ciangin awging khatin a nihveina hopihkik a, “Pasian in siang hi a cihte nekhuailo hi ci kei in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Hih bangin thumvei a cih khit ciangin tua hong kikhaisuk na vantung ah a kilatokik hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Peter in a mangmuhna a khiatna bang hi ding hiam ci a, lungmang in a om laitak in Simon inn a zongzong Cornelius sawltakte kongpi mai ah a ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Amaute in, “Hihlai ah Peter a kici Simon hong tung kha hiam?” ci in a galdot uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Peter in a mangmuhna ngaihsun in a om laitak in Kha in ama kiangah, “En in, mi thum in nang hong zong uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Tua mite keima hong sawl ahi hi. Lunghianglo tak in amaute zui in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Tua ciangin Cornelius in a hong sawl mite kiangah Peter paisuk a, “Hong en un, na mi zon uh keimah ka hi hi. Amah in Pasian a kihta, a thuman mi khat hi a, Judah minam buppi in a zahtak uh mi khat ahi hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Tua ciangin Peter in inn sungah amaute samin a giaksak hi. Tu in Cornelius in a tanaute le a lawm itteng kaikhawm in amaute a ngak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Inn sungah Peter a lut ciangin Cornelius in dawn a, a khe phungah bokin a bia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Ahih hangin Peter in amah phongto a, “Ding in, kei zong mihing mah ka hi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Peter in amah a hopih kawmin inn sungah a lut ciangin mi tampi kikhawm in a om a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Tua ciangin Peter in amaute kiangah, “Judah mi khat minam dangte tawh a kikholh ding le a kianga a hawh ding thukham tawh kituak lo hi cih thu na thei uh hi. Tua ciangin puanpak a silh mi khat ka mai ah hong dinga,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">‘Cornelius aw, na thungetnate Pasian in hong zazo a, mizawngte na huhna zong a hong ciaptehsak zo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tua ahih manin Joppa khua ah mi sawl inla, Peter a kici Simon samsak in. Amah in tuipi gei‑a a teeng savun bawlpa Simon inn ah zintung in a om hi. Amah hong tun ciangin thu hong gen ding hi,’ a hong ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Tua ahih manin nang hong sam ding mi kong sawl pah a, tu in hong paithei na hih manin hoih mahmah hi.     "12": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">12</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua hun sungin Herod kumpipa in pawlpi mite pawlkhat bawlsiat dingin a man hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Amah in John sanggampa James namsau tawh a thatsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua thu in Judah mite lungdamsak hi cih a muh ciangin Peter zong mat dingin a sawm leuleu hi. Tua hunin Silngo Sawhloh Anlum Pawi sung ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Amah in Peter a mat khit ciangin thongah khum a, Paisan Pawi a ven ciangin mihonpi mai ah a lahkhiat dingin galkap li ta in a om pawl lite cin dingin a ap hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua ahih manin thong sungah Peter kikhum a, ahi zongin pawlpi in ama aa dingin tatsat loin Pasian kiangah thu a ngetsak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Herod in Peter a lahkhiat sawm ni zanin sikkhau nih tawh amah kikhih a, galkap nihte kikal ah a ihmu hi. Tua kongpi ama thu in kihong a, amaute gel zong a pusuakkhia uh hi. Kongzing khat a zuih khit uh ciangin vantungmi in thakhat in amah a nusia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Peter in khua a phawkkik ciangin, “Tu in Topa in a vantungmi hong sawlin, Herod khut sung pan le Judah mite hong thah nading panin hong honkhia khinzo hi cih thu teltak in ka thei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Peter in hih thu a phawk khit ciangin Mark a kici John nu Mary inn ah va pai a, tualai ah mi tampi thungen in a kikhawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Peter in kong a kiuh ciangin Rhoda kici numeino khat kong a hon dingin a pai hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tua nu in Peter aw ahihlam a theih ciangin lungdamlua a, kongpi hon nai loin inn sungah lehtaikik a, kongpi mai ah Peter a dinlam a va ko hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Ahih hangin amaute in, “A hai hi ni teh!” a ci uh hi. Kum thum tawntung sun le zan tatsat loin khitui tawh note khempeuh tunga kong hilh thute na phawk un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">“Tu in sanggamte aw, Pasian tung le ama hehpihna thu ah note kong ap hi. Ama hehpihna thu in note hong kipsak in a sianthosak mi khempeuh tawh luahna a hong ngahkhawmsak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Kham le ngun, nikteen puansilh kuama a ka deihgawh ngei kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Hi hi, keimah le ka lawmte kisapna teng hih ka khut in hong guan hi cih no mahmah in zong na thei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">Na khempeuh ah hih bangin nasep hahkat in a zawngkhal mite na huh nadingun kong lak khinzo hi. ‘Ngahna sangin piakkhiatna ah thupha om zaw hi,’ ci a, Topa Zeisu thugente na phawk un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">Hih thuteng a gen khit ciangin khukdin in amaute khempeuh tawh thu a ngenkhawm hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"37\"><sup data-verseid=\"37\">&nbsp;<!-- -->37<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"37\">Tua ciangin a vekpi un nakpitak in kap uha Paul ngawngkawi in a nam uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"38\"><sup data-verseid=\"38\">&nbsp;<!-- -->38<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"38\">Ka maitang nong mu nawn kei ding uh hi a cihna thu in amaute a dahsak phadiak hi. tua khuavak a muh uh ciangin a lau uh hi. Ahi zongin kei hong kihopihna awging a tel thei kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">“Tua ciangin keimah in, ‘Topa aw, bang hih ding ka hi hiam?’ ka ci hi. “Topa in, ‘Tho inla, Damascus khuapi sungah lut in. Nangma sep dinga ka gelsate tualai ah kong hilh ding hi,’ a hong ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Tua khuavak khauhlua a, khua mu theilo ka hih manin ka lawmte in hong bankaih uh a, Damascus khuapi ka tung hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">“Tualai ah thukham tawh kituak in Pasian a bia, Ananias kici mi khat om a, tua khua‑a teeng Judah mi khempeuh in a zahtak mahmah khat uh ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Amah ka kiangah hong pai in ka gei ah hong dinga, ‘Sanggampa Saul aw, khua muta in,’ a hong cih ciangin tua hun lian mahin amah ka mu thei pah hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Pasian deihna a thei ding, Midikpa a mu ding le ama thu genna aw a za dingin i pute i pate Pasian in nang hong teel zo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Na muh khitsa le na zak khitsa thute mi khempeuh tungah na gen dinga, ama aa dingin teci na pang ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Tu in zong bang ngak na hi hiam? Tho inla tui kiphum in. Topa minin thungen inla, na mawhnate silsiang in,’ a hong ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">“Tua khit ciangin Jerusalem khuapi ah ciahkik in biakinnpi huang sungah thungen a ka om laitak in mang ka mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tua ka mangmuhna sungah Topa ka mu a, amah in, ‘Kinawh inla Jerusalem khuapi pan paikhia mengmeng in. Banghang hiam cihleh keima thu teci na panna amaute in hong sang lo ding uh hi,’ a hong ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">“Tua ciangin keimah in, ‘Topa aw, kikhopna inn sungah lutin nang hong um mite satin thongah ka khiatna thu amaute in a hong thei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Nangma thu hanga thahna a thuak Stephen sisan a luansak laitak un ama sih nading thukim in amaute kiangah ka dinga, amah a that mite puan zong ka kepsak hi,’ ka ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">“Tua ciangin amah in, ‘Hih mun pan paikhia in. Gamlapi a om Gentile‑te kiangah kong sawl ding hi,’ a hong ci hi,” ci in a gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Amaute in Paul thugen hih ciangciang a ngai uh hi. Tua khit ciangin a aw uh sangsak in, “Hih bang mipa leitung panin hemkhia un a nungta dingin kilawm lo hi!” ci in a kiko uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">A kiko kawmun a puante uh suahkhia in vantung lamah leivui a thehto uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Galkapte in galkap lenah Paul a paipih nadingun galkap mangpaɠ in thu a pia hi. Banghang in mihonpi in amah langpan in hi bangin kiko uh hi ding hiam cih a theih nadingin amah sata thu a sit nadingun a sawl hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Amaute in savun khau tawh amah a hen laitak un Paul in ama kianga a ding galkap 100 ukpa kiangah, “Rome gam mi khat mawh hi ci a, thukhenna om nailopi a sat ding pen thukhenna ngeina tawh a kituak mah ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Galkap 100 ukpa in hih thu a zak ciangin galkap mangpaɠ kiangah pai in, “Hihpa Rome gam mi ahi hi na hihsawm thu kidawm in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Tua ciangin Paul kiangah galkap mangpaɠ pai in, “Nang, Rome gam mi na hi hiam hong gen in,” a ci hi. Paul in, “Ka hi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Tua ciangin galkap mangpaɠ in, “Ken Rome gam mi ka suah nadingin sum tampi ka pia hi,” a ci hi. Paul in, “Kei ka suahpih ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Tua ciangin thu a sitsawm mite ama kiang panin a kihemkhia pah uh hi. Galkap mangpaɠ in Paul na hen kha khinzo ahih manin Rome gam mi ahihlam a theih ciangin a lau hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Banghang in Judah mite in Paul mawhmat uh hiam cih thu galkap mangpa in theitel nuam ahih manin a zingciang in Paul a kihennate a phelsak hi. Siampi liante le thukhenteɠ khempeuh kikhawmsak a, Paul zong paipih in amaute mai ah a koih nadingun thu a pia hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "23": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">23</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua ciangin Paul in thukhenteɠ limtak in a etkawm in, “Ute naute aw, tuni dongin Pasian mai ah kisuang hetlo in ka nungta hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tua ciangin Siampi Ukpa Ananias in Paul kianga a ding mite kiangah Paul muk a satsak nadingun thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ciangin Paul in ama kiangah, “Leikang kizut suangcian tawh a kibang pa aw, Pasian in nang hong sat ding hi! Banghang hiam cihleh thukham tawh kituak in thu hong khen dingin a tu kimlai banghang in thukham tawh kilehbulh in kei hong satsak na hi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua kima a ding mite in, “Pasian Siampi Ukpa zahko vial ding na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua ciangin Paul in, “Sanggamte aw, amah Siampi Ukpa ahihlam ka thei kei hi. Lai Siangtho in, ‘Na mite a ukpa gensia kei in ci mah hi,’ ” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Amaute pawlkhat Sadducee pawlte hi uh a, a dangte Pharisee pawlte ahihlam uh Paul in a theih ciangin thukhenteɠ mai ah kiko a, “Ute naute aw, Pharisee mipa khat tapa Pharisee pawlte khat ka hi hi. Misite thawhkikna thu tawh kisai lametna hangin thusitna a thuak ka hi hi!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Tua bang a cih ciangin Pharisee pawlte le Sadducee pawlte kisel uh a, mihonpi pawl nih a suak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Banghang hiam cihleh Sadducee pawlte in misite thokik lo hi, vantungmi om lo hi, kha zong om lo hi a ci uh hi. Ahih hangin Pharisee pawlte in a nih in om hi ci in a um uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Tua ciangin amaute nakpi in a kiko uh hi. Pharisee pawlte sunga thukhamhilh siate hong ding uh a, “Hihpa tungah thusia ka mu kei uh hi. Vantungmi khat ahih keileh kha khatpeuh in hopih ahih leh Pasian langpan in i do kei ding hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Tu in kipawlkhenna le kitotna nasialua ahih manin Paul a tum a tel a suahkhak ding uh galkap mangpaɠ a patau hi. Tua ahih ciangin galkapte paisuksak in mihonpite lak panin thatanghat suangin Paul kaikhia a, galkap lenah a paipih nadingun thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">A zingciang zanin Paul kiangah Topa dinga, “Paul aw, lungkia kei in. Keima aa dingin Jerusalem khuapi ah teci na pan bangin Rome khuapi ah zong na panglai ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Khua a vak ciangin Judah mite pawlkhat kituah uh a, Paul a thah khit mateng un an ne lo tui dawn lo dingin a kiciam uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tu in Paul a thahsawm mite 40 val a pha uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Siampi liante le makai vaihawmte kiangah amaute va pai uh a, “Paul ka thah khit mateng un bangmah ne lo dingin ka kiciam khinzo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tua ahih manin note le thukhenteɠ in Paul thu a kicing zaw in a sit nuam bang khatin zingciang in a hong paipih nadingun galkap mangpaɠ kiangah va gen un. Note kianga hong tunpihma un a that dingin kigingsa in ka na om ding uh hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Ahih hangin Paul sanggamnu tapa in tua mite suamsim nading thu a zak ciangin galkap lenah va lutin Paul kiangah a va ko hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua ciangin Paul in galkap 100 ukte khat sam a, “Hih tangvalpa in galkap mangpaɠ kiangah gennop khat nei ahih manin ama kiangah va puak in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tua pa in galkap mangpaɠ kiangah amah a paipih hi. Tua ciangin amah in, “Thongkiapa Paul in kei hong sam a, hih tangvalpa nang kianga kong paipih ding hong ngen hi. Tangvalpa in nang kiangah gennop khat hong nei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Tua ciangin galkap mangpaɠ in a khut tawh kai in paikhiatpih a, “Nong gennop thu bang ahi hiam?” ci in a dongsim hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Tangvalpa in, “Judah mite in a kicing zaw a Paul thu a sit nuam bang khatin zingciang in thukhenteɠ kiangah amah na paisak nading hong ngen dingin a kithukim khinzo uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Amaute thu mang kei in. Banghang hiam cihleh Paul a thah khit mateng un an ne lo tui dawn lo dingin a kiciam khinsa mihing 40 val in amah a pangsim uh hi. Tu in amaute in na kamciam piak ding bek ngakin kigingsa in a om uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Tua ciangin galkap mangpaɠ in tangvalpa ciahsak a, “Hih thute kei nong hilh lam kuama kiangah gen kei in,” ci in thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Tua ciangin amah in galkap 100 ukte nih sam a, “Zan nai thum ciangin Caesarea khua donga a pai dingin galkap 200, sakol galkap 70 le teipi a tawi galkap 200 kithawisak un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Paul a tuan nading khat zong keng unla, mangpipa Felix kiangah hoihtak in va puak un,” ci in thu a pia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Amah in hih bangin laikhak khat a gelh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Keimah Claudius Lysias in a lian mahmah mangpipa Felix kong hopih hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Judah mite in hihpa manin thah a sawm uh hi. Amah Rome gam mi khat ahihlam ka theih ciangin galkapte tawh pai in ka va honkhia hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Amah a mawhmatna uh thei nuam ka hih manin amaute thukhenteɠ kiangah ka puak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">Amaute thukham tawh kisai kinialna hangin a mawhmat uh hi a, sih nading le thongkiat nading zah dong ama mawhna ka mu kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Judah mite in amah pangsim uh hi cih thu a hong kigen ciangin nang kiangah kong puak pah hi. A mawhmat mite in a mawhmatna uh nangma mai ah hong sun nadingun thu ka pia zo hi. Mangpha, ci in lai a khak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Tua ciangin galkapte in a thu ngahna uh tawh kizui in Paul lakhia uh a, Antipatris khua ah a zan a zan in a paipih uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">A zingciang in Paul tawh a paikhawm dingin sakol galkap teng omlai uh a, galkap dangteng galkap lenah a ciahkik uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Caesarea khua a tun uh ciangin mangpipa khutah laikhak pia uh a, Paul zong ama khutah a ap uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"34\">Mangpipa in laikhak a sim khit ciangin Paul kiangah, “Bang gam mi na hi hiam?” ci in a dong hi. Cilicia gam mi ahihlam a theih ciangin,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"35\"><sup data-verseid=\"35\">&nbsp;<!-- -->35<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"35\">“Nang hong mawhmat mite a hong tun uh ciangin na thu kong sit ding hi,” a ci hi.     "26": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">26</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua khit ciangin Agrippa in Paul kiangah, “Na thu tawh kisai na gen theih nading hun kong pia hi,” a ci hi.
